	$(document).ready(function() {
	
		// Fetch stickers
		if($('body').find('.sticker_container.unfetched').length > 0) {
			if($('body').find('.campaignContentWrapper').length <= 0) {
				CatalogServices.fetchStickers($('.emarketingspot'));
			}
			
			if($('body').find('.additionalProducts').length > 0) {
				CatalogServices.fetchStickers($('.additionalProducts'));
			}
		}

		
			$.ajaxPrefilter(function(options, originalOptions, jqXHR) {
				if (!/^http(s)?:.*$/.test(options.url)) {
					options.url = "http://www.stark-suomi.fi/requestURI?".replace("requestURI?", options.url);
				}
			});
		
		
		$(".info_dialog_link").info_dialog_link({
			closeButtonText : MessageDisplay.getMessage("general.close")
		});

		$(document).on(CustomEvents.gridChanged, function() {
			$("img.product_image").productimage();
		});

		$("img.product_image").productimage();

		// SUB CATEGORY TOGGLE
	    $('.subCategorySlider').click(function() {
	          $(this).next('ul').toggle();
	          $(this).toggleClass('open');
	    });

	    // CONTENT PAGE SUB PAGE TOGGLE
	    $('.content-nav .nuoli').click(function() {
	          $(this).parent('h2').next('ul').toggle();
	          $(this).toggleClass('open');
	    });

	    // FRONTPAGE BIG SLIDER
	    $('.frontpage #big-slider').slick({
	    	dots: true,
			autoplay: true,
			autoplaySpeed: 6000,
	    });
	    
	    $('.frontpage #marketing-popup-close').click(function(){
    		$.cookie("marketing_banner", true , { domain: '', path: '' });
    		$('.frontpage #marketing-popup-wrapper').fadeOut(200);
    		$('body').css("overflow", "");
    		$('#marketing-popup-wrapper').css("overflow", "hidden");
		});
	    
	    if($("#marketing-popup").children().length > 2 && $.cookie("marketing_banner") == null && $('#marketing_popup_value').text() == 'true'){
    		
	    	$('.frontpage #marketing-popup-wrapper').delay(MessageDisplay.getMessage("general.marketing.timeup")).fadeIn(200, function(){
	    		$('body').css("overflow", "hidden");
    			$('#marketing-popup-wrapper').css("overflow", "auto");
	    		if($('#subscribe-background').is(':visible')){
	    			$('#subscribe-background').hide();
	    		}
	    	});
	    }
	    
	    if($("#subscribe-content").children().length > 3 && $.cookie("newsletter_banner") == null && $('#newsletter_popup_value').text() == 'true'){
    		
    		setTimeout(function() {
    			if(!$('#subscribe-background').is(':visible')){
	    			$('#subscribe-background').fadeIn(150);
	    			$('body').css("overflow", "hidden");
	    			$('#subscribe-background').css("overflow", "auto");
	    		}
    		}, MessageDisplay.getMessage("general.marketing.timeup"));
	    }

	    // FRONTPAGE PRODUCT THUMBNAIL SLIDER
	    $('.frontpage #slider_tuotenostot_etusivu_spotti').slick({

		$('#marketing-squares .slider').slick({

	    	slidesToScroll: 3,

		if(($(this).scrollTop() + $(window).height()) < ($('#footer_page').offset().top)){
			$('#subscribe-popup-wrapper').addClass('sticky');
		}

	    $(document).scroll(function () {

		    var y = $(this).scrollTop() + $(window).height();
		    var footerPos = $('#footer_page').offset().top;
		    
		    if (y < footerPos) {
		        $('#subscribe-popup-wrapper').addClass('sticky');
		        
		    } else {
		    	if(!$('#subscribe-background').is(':visible')){
		        	$('#subscribe-popup-wrapper').removeClass('sticky');
		        }
		    }
		});
		
		$('#subscribe-popup-close').click(function(){
			$.cookie("newsletter_banner", true , { domain: '', path: '' });
    		$('#subscribe-background').fadeOut(150);
    		$('body').css("overflow", "");

		});

	    $('#subscribe-popup-wrapper').click(function(){
	    	if(!$('#subscribe-background').is(':visible')){
    			$('#subscribe-background').fadeIn(150);
    			$('body').css("overflow", "hidden");
    			$('#subscribe-background').css("overflow", "auto");
    		}
		});
		
		$('.dropdown-top').click( function() {
        	$(this).next().toggle();
    	});
    	
    	$('.dropdown-option li').click( function() {
        	$('.dropdown-top').html($(this).html());
        	$('#modclass').val($(this).attr('id'));
    	});
    	
    	
    	
    	$('#subscribe-background').click( function(e) {
    			if(!$('.dropdown-option').is(e.target) && !$('.dropdown-top').is(e.target)){
    				$('.dropdown-option').hide();
    			}
    	});
    	
    	
	    
	    // MOBILE SIDENAV
	    $('.mobile-control').on('click', function() {
	    	$(this).toggleClass('open');
	    });

	    // CLOSE FACETS NAV ON SELECTION
	    $('.campaign .facets a').on('click', function() {
	    	$('.mobile-control').removeClass('open');
	    });

	    // SERVICE DROPDOWN
	    $('.service_dropdown_head').on('click', function() {
	    	var painike = $(this).find('button');
	    	$(this).toggleClass('open');

	    	if ($(this).is('.open')) {
	    		painike.text('Piilota');
	    	} else {
	    		painike.text('Näytä');
	    	}

	    });

	    // SUBSCRIBE FORM INIT
	    SubscribeForm.init();

		// PRODUCT THUMBNAILS must be initialized
		var options = {
			wishlist_buttons: 'article.product .wishlist', 
		    addtocart_buttons: 'article.product .btn_tocart'
		 };
	    
	    ProductThumbnail.init(options);

	    if (!/android|iphone|ipod|series60|symbian|windows ce|blackberry/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
    		$("a[rel^='lightbox']").slimbox({}, null, function(el) {
    			return (this == el) || ((this.rel.length > 8) && (this.rel == el.rel));
    		});
	    }
	});

		(function($) {
		$.sanitize = function(input) {
		var output = input.replace(/[&<>\/]/g, '');
	    return output;
		};
	})(jQuery);

	$(function() {
		$('#button_search').click(function() {
			var $input = $('#field_search').val();
			$('#field_search').val($.sanitize($input));
		});
	});
	
	// Do after page load
	$("document").ready(function(){

		var $search_input = $('#field_search'); 
		
		var autoSuggest = $search_input.autosuggest({ 
		
		  serviceUrl:'AjaxSearchAutoSuggestData',		    
		  minChars: 3, // min chars to start suggest
		  deferRequestBy: 200, //miliseconds
		  //submitButton: "#button_search",
		  autoSubmit: true, // submit form when user clicks on selection
		  noCache: true, //default is false, set to true to disable caching
		  
		  //additional parameters
		  params: {
		  	count:'10', // max suggested keywords
			storeId: "10151",
			catalogId: "10051",
			masterCatalogId: "10001",
			langId: "-11"
		  },
		  // Translations
		  translations: {
    		suggestedKeyWords: "Hakusanat",
    		brand: "Tuotemerkit",
    		category: "Kategoriat",
    		history: "Historia"	  
		  } 
		});		
		
		$('#button_search').click(function(e) {
			// check for empty input
			if(!$search_input.val()) {
				$search_input.blur();
				e.preventDefault();
			}
		});
	});
</script>

<!-- end GA code for chat --><!-- begin Chat system code -->
<script type="text/javascript">
  (function() {
    var se = document.createElement('script'); se.type = 'text/javascript'; se.async = true;
    se.src = '//storage.googleapis.com/code.snapengage.com/js/9c0f5f6c-df19-47f3-94f2-8d2cb849ed9f.js';
    var done = false;
    se.onload = se.onreadystatechange = function() {
      if (!done&&(!this.readyState||this.readyState==='loaded'||this.readyState==='complete')) {
        done = true;
	var seAgent;
		SnapABug.setCallback('OpenProactive', function(agent, msg) {
			seAgent = agent;
			ga('SSETracker.send','event','ChatProaktiivinen', 'Tarjottu asiakkaalle', seAgent);
			});
		SnapABug.setCallback('StartChat', function(email, msg, type) {
		    if (type == 'proactive') {
        	ga('SSETracker.send','event','ChatProaktiivinen', 'Asiakas vastasi', seAgent);
    		}
			if (type == 'manual') {
        	ga('SSETracker.send','event','ChatManuaalinen', 'Chat aloitettu', seAgent);
    		}
			});
		SnapABug.setCallback('Open', function(status) {
			ga('SSETracker.send','event','ChatManuaalinen', 'Chat-valikko avattu',status);
			});
		SnapEngage.setCallback('MessageSubmit', function (email, msg) {
			ga('SSETracker.send','event','ChatOffline', 'Offline-viesti');
			});		
		SnapEngage.setCallback('Close', function (type, status) {
			if (type == 'form') {
        	ga('SSETracker.send','event','ChatClosed', 'Lomake suljettu',status);
    		}
			if (type == 'chat') {
        	ga('SSETracker.send','event','ChatClosed', 'Chat suljettu',status);
			}
			if (type == 'proactive') {
        	ga('SSETracker.send','event','ChatClosed', 'Proaktiivinen suljettu',status);
			}
			});
		SnapEngage.setCallback('ChatMessageSent', function (msg) {
			ga('SSETracker.send','event','ChatKeskustelu', 'Asiakas kirjoitti viestin');
			});
		SnapEngage.setCallback('StartCallme', function (phone) {
			ga('SSETracker.send','event','ChatCallMe', 'CallMe',phone);
			});
		SnapEngage.setCallback('ChatMessageReceived', function (agent, msg) {
			seAgent=agent;
			var date = new Date();
			date.setTime(date.getTime() + (30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
			document.cookie = 'chatWith=' + encodeURIComponent(agent) + '; expires=' + date.toGMTString() + '; path=/;';
			ga('SSETracker.send','event','ChatKeskustelu', 'Agentti kirjoitti viestin',seAgent);
			}); 
		}
    };
    var s = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0]; s.parentNode.insertBefore(se, s);
  })();
</script>
<!-- end Chat system code -->
